< review>
Been to the Walnut Creek one. This location is not as nice. Maybe it was because it was close to 10 pm. The chocolate chip and the Mac nut white chocolate cookies were not warm and kind of tough as I bit into my Rocky Road ice cream sandwich. Plus, the Rocky Road was hard. Had to chew because the normally warm cookies would have soften the ice cream to bring out the flavors. Couldn't really taste the chocolate, marshmallows or nuts.

The price is the same at $3 without topping which is a great price if the custom-made ice cream sandwich was great.

Hubby liked his Banana Fosters ice cream sandwich. He could taste the bananas and caramel. His Mac nut cookies were barely warm too. Only saving grace - there was no line - since we were there late.</review>

< Review>
Fun idea of ice cream sandwiches where you can choose your cookies and ice cream. Liked that you can have different cookies on either side, and the cookies were pretty good, especially as they warm them up so the ice cream sort of melts, which is messy but delicious! Normally I find ice cream sandwiches too solid as the cookies are frozen too, so these were very good. The one negative of this store was the service though. One staff member, who took her sweet time about everything... It took us almost 20 mins to get served, and there was only one family in front of us. So while I like the idea of made to order ice cream sandwiches, I'd suggest they find a more efficient delivery mechanism!<//Review>

<Review>I give them credit for the concept plus the smell of the cookies travels about a block each way so it is extremely tempting.  However, they have a few design issues to address.  The cookies are too hot and the ice cream too soft and it ends up being a mess by the third bite and only getting worse.  You cant really enjoy the experience when you are trying to eat and not have everything drip on you.  Perhaps, scoop the ice cream and give it a quick freeze and then place in between cookies or perhaps, lower the temperature of the cookies.  Just some thoughts.  Good concept, execution needs a little improvement<//Review>< pics>

To start, I can't really understand how anyone can give a place that serves cookie ice cream sandwiches less than 5 stars. So clearly I am biased. Things to know,

It is now $4 for one ice cream sandwich and one topping is no longer included (will cost you $.75 each)
You can mix and match your cookies before they warm in the oven + 1 one ice cream choice
Suggest you split in half and share unless you have a huge sweet tooth

Overall Thoughts

<review>Amazing ice-cream and tons of flavor combinations!< /review><pictures>None< /pictures><Response>{'time': 1486056350422, 'text': 'HI, thanks for the awesome 5 stars rating. We look forward to serving you again.'}<//Response>< gmapID>
0x808f9e70c13de767:0xbce51ad2040dde55< /gmapID>
</record>
</dataset><record>
< resp>
{'time': 1460103301058, 'text': 'Thanks for sharing your recent experience with us. We look forward to serving you again.'}</resp>
< text>
You know that irresistible aroma of fresh-baked cookies that flows in the air and wafts past your nose making you stop in your step and wonder, "where is that delicious scent coming from?" Yea, that's how Cream entices you into their store. I was able to resist the first time I came to the area, just buying Gong Cha and leaving. But when I came with my family, my sister was unable to resist the tempting aroma of cookies and made it her mission to get an ice cream sandwich cookie before we headed back to LA. And I followed her inside since the smell of cookies was just too amazing.

So Cream has a wide assortment of freshly baked cookies as well as a good number of ice cream flavors and toppings to do any sort of combination/creation that your heart desires. You can get cookies by itself, ice cream by itself, make an ice cream cookie sandwich, add toppings, make a premium ice cream cookie sandwich, make sundaes, make a taco (3 ice cream flavors and 2 toppings), purchase brownies, buy milkshakes, or get a coffee drink. Yep, the menu is pretty extensive. So if you want to make some sort of ice cream cookie concoction, chances are the workers at Cream will help you out.

I tried the butter sugar cookie on its own while my sister got a snickerdoodle salted caramel ice cream sandwich. The cookies individually weren't too expensive - like around a dollar or so for each, and they were taken right out of the oven! The butter sugar cookie was a bit of a let down in that it was way too sweet. I couldn't finish the entire cookie because the flavor was a bit too cloying. It reminded me a lot of the sugar cookies from Ralph's, which .. meh, are decent but not the best.

The moment I heard my sister order the ice cream sandwich, I knew she wouldn't finish it. And I was right! The combination was way too sweet. The snickerdoodle cookies were amazing. Still warm from the oven, it tasted like cinnamon and sugar - bliss! The salted caramel ice cream was also good - by itself. It's definitely nowhere near as good as Bi-Rite's. Mixed with the cookie and it was really sweet. And I like sweet things, but this was too much. We couldn't finish the cookie sandwich and had to toss some of it in the trash, which was really sad. However, price for this wasn't too bad - around $3-$4 and I think there was a check in offer.

tl;dr - Workers are fairly nice. This shop is definitely a good place to go if you're in the mood for a quick dessert or treat. Everything is clean, there are plenty of tables, the storefront is amazing, and the smell of cookies will draw you in! I would recommend trying the flavors of ice cream first before combining it with a cookie because these concoctions can get super sweet! I would just order cookies and ice cream separately, but that's just me. Glad I got to try Cream and it's good to know that there are locations in SoCal that I can easily visit. I rarely get a craving for ice cream, so if anything I will be back for the cookies!< /text>

<time>1599613423563<//time><user_id>118133936986782764436<//user_id><Review>Interesting idea. This place seems to be very progressive. Health conscious. And environmentally friendly.

First thing I noticed is you order on a touch screen (normally might be a good idea but now since we have a pandemic, I wish there was better reassurance that it was a clean screen.)

Second,  it's completely cashless. No cash. That does hypothetically cut down on a lot of potential problems including sanitation, robbery, and it could also hire people with low credit (most businesses won't hire people with bad credit when there's money handing involved.)

It is a very simple menu (almost too simple. I'm thinking they will add things in the future but for now...) I just ordered a burger. But they also have a chicken sandwich and an impossible burger. You can choose between regular bun, whole wheat, or a lettuce bun. Then you choose every topping. There's nothing unique for toppings. Very basic. Ketchup, mustard, onions, lettuce, tomato, pickles mayonnaise, an aoili, which I'm guessing was some type of hot sauce or Chipotle possibly because it was orange red colored. Nothing too crazy. And a few types of cheese. Just very simple choices.

I added air fried fries but they also have air fried sweet potato fries. It is healthier eating without using oil to fry but I might take awhile getting used to this type because they do not stay warm for long and the texture is slightly pasty and limp. It is satisfying knowing I didn't eat fried foods. I guess...

Finally, I added a chocolate shake which was basically a Wendy's frosty. Except it had a little more of a homemade feeling to it. Really good. I love frostys. (Straws are paper)

Overall not bad. The positives are the health conscious and for fast food, I do like the cashless checkout. The negatives would be the selection. I mean, if it's just a burger on the menu, I want the burger to be extraordinary. It was very low price and fast and friendly but I'm almost wishing it was a seasoned slider or 3. I do like simplicity and I can see the direction they are going is steering away from junk fast food and making healthier fast food but I just think that with so much competition, I need a little more of a signature on it. I almost feel guilty for saying that because to agree would be the problems that other countries see with Americans about how good, decent, food just isn't enough. Everything in America has to be kicked up a notch.</Review><Gmap_id>0x80db7fddf6c4d479:0x313a8a157e79d4e5< /Gmap_id>< pictures>

<Date>1602560400677<//Date><rate>3</rate><Review>Randomly found this place looking for a place to eat.  It is burger joint that reminds me of Sonic or Rally's but a whole lot better.  Place is strictly drive thru or walk up service.  No inside seating.  I do not remember seeing any tables outside.  You pull in and place your order via touch screen.  Pull up close to the curb or it is a little hard to reach.  I love how you can customize your order without worrying if the server can understand you over the speaker phone.  It is strictly card only.  You pay at the kiosk and remember the number that flashes on the screen.  The kiosk is very similar to what many of the fast food locations are adopting.  You pull up, state your number, and they hand over the food.

The night I stopped in, the gentleman checking the kiosk was very friendly and helpful.

The burger was really good.  It is not huge but very good.  Fries were ok.  Compared to my ideal fry, it was a step up from ok.

I was really impressed with the set up.  It is set up to be quick and efficient.  One hick up I fore see is large orders where you have to manually enter multiple entries, some one who is not familiar with touch screen, or some one who is very undecided on what they want to order and just stares at the screen.

Overall, well worth it.< /Review><Pictures>None</Pictures>< Response>

Went today for the first time and had a good experience. No wait for the kiosk. Love that we could take our time to order for our family of 5 without having to yell through a speaker. It was a little laggy and I think they could streamline the process to make ordering a bit quicker. I appreciated that they provided gloves. They didn't have some items, no POG or shakes or guacamole yet. Our food came out quickly, but like others have said, the fries were cold. I think they need a way to get their food hotter. I thought my burger was pretty good. Nothing amazing, but I like the eco-friendly attitude of the company and the low prices so I feel it was fine for the money. I wish their website had nutrition information. My daughter didn't like the bacon she had on her burger- said it was too "smoky". I hope they take these criticisms and improve some of their processes. All-in-all it was a good experience for a new fast food place and I'm sure we'll be back.</review>

< review>
I recently visited the newest location in Oceanside, CA (Oceanside Blvd) with my Autistic daughter, who had been talking non stop about placing her order. She had memorized the entire menu and knew exactly which sauces to try.

We order through drive through, and confirm which sauces we wanted. Drive up window I encountered 3 employees with theirs backs facing me while waiting to be acknowledged for 2-3 minutes.

Get home to enjoy the meal and no SAUCE was provided in our take out. Not that it‚Äôs a big deal but it kinda is because what makes these different from every other place serving fried chicken is there special Louisiana sauces!

If anyone has met an Autistic person you can feel my pain about trying to explain why there is no sauce :( and yes I could have drove back, walked in and complained but I went through drive thru for a reason!

Disappointed special needs Mom< /review>

1612215338302< /Time>
<rating>1< /rating><Review>There's no such thing as fast food when it comes to any Popeyes that I've ever been to in Southern California; especially this location. This place has lines as long as In-N-Out, and this place is about 3x slower than In-N-Out. Expect to wait 30 to 50 minutes for your order, even without tons of cars in line. Ive gone multiple times because I do love the food and price; however the wait is extremely frustrating and many times I still find myself thinking that it wasnt worth the wait. Don't think that Im being just unreasonable because this location is new...they pulled staff from other Popeyes who were already trained up and it's still unacceptably slow. I dont understand why Popeyes cant keep up with making a lot of food in advance and keeping it warm and fresh (somehow?) in order to keep cars moving through the drive-thru at a much faster pace. KFC can pull off faster cooking so why can't Popeyes? I get that KFC isnt as high quality as Popeyes, but still...there has to be a way for these guys to get orders out faster. If I owned this business I'd be looking into ways to drastically improve production, because it should be clear to any business owner that frustrated customers leads to a decline in repeat sales, and long-lines scare people away, and this means LESS SALES. Popeyes slogan of "Louisiana-Fast" has me thinking the phrase is more of an ironic joke than anything truthful. Louisiana-Fast must mean "half-speed" for the rest of us... Do I expect McDonalds speed? No. But do I expect to wait in line for 50 minutes when there's only 6 cars ahead if me? NO. If great tasting and affordable food is worth it to you and you have no place to be while having no idea how long you'll be stuck in line without being able to quickly leave if youre running low on gas or need to use the restroom...then try it out! It honestly is great food. They really need to fix their production time though; and that's an issue for every local Popeyes around this area. I've been to Popeyes in other states and they're super fast...so maybe its a regional training issue that badly needs attention.</Review>< pics>

I was at Gourmet Artisan Fine Sandwiches on April 12th. I had the Blue Burger which came on a tray with a cute newspaper deli wrap. The food was great but the newspaper wrap was atrocious.

The paper was dated November 19, 1989 and on its front page boasted the following articles:  The Berlin Wall Falls, Remarkable Upset in Olympic History, Titanic Found, and a crossword puzzle.

The only event that happened in November of 89 was the Berlin Wall falling. US over Soviet Olympic hockey game was in 1980 (Olympics happen on EVEN years), The Titanic was found in 1985; a little late to the party on these stories. The crossword would have been fine except for the following clues: Across 11: "____ Doubtfire" and Down 18: Sandler of "Big Daddy" Surely they could have come up with more appropriate 1989 clues to get us to the answers "Mrs" and "Adam".

Gourmet Artisan Fine Sandwiches is Fake News!< /review>

Stopped in to get a bite while waiting for a tour shuttle. I felt bad because the guy working was literally alone. He was taking orders (phone and counter) and cooking. He worked that place like  boss and did so with a pleasant demeanor! I had no expectations, but this is arguably the best burgers that I have ever had. The meat was fresh and well seasoned. The fries....OMG the fries! I had half sweet potato and half burgerim fries which were sliced like chips. They both were the perfect texture. I would love for this place to branch out to Texas (specifically Austin üòÅ).  I would plan a day just for the burgers and fries.< /text>

101050019728863492658< /user>
<username>MrMoruss78 Mo</username><Time>1537130243556< /Time><Rating>5<//Rating>< Review>
Wow! Super surprised with the quality of meat, flavors, and service.

Walking in a I didn't expect much from this strip mall set up.  Place was pretty empty besides the fact that there were plenty of workers.

I was perplexed with the menu ordering. 2 burgers for $6.99? Or three for $9.99? But my questions were answered when I received my order and found that they were sliders.  At that moment I felt annoyed and disappointed at the same time.

First slider up, the Murguez. A beef slider seasoned for various spices topped with pepper jack cheese, salad and jalape√±os. Bursting with flavor I was ecstatic on how juicy and delicious this little Burger was. Suddenly, I felt slightly less annoyed.  Second up, the 28 day dry aged beef slider. Again, this little slider surprised me.  The little twang from the aged beef and California toppings ( Swiss cheese, avocado, lettuce and tomato) adds the perfect touch to this Burger.

Added bonus: buy $10 worth of food and get 4 delectable pieces of chicken wings/Nuggets with your order. Trust me. These chicken wings can stand on their own vs any chicken wing joint.  Don't know  how long this is going to last. Come check them out!!<//Review>

< review>
Can't say enough about local fixture.  I'm in here pretty much on the daily to pick up a drink at the coffee bar.  Their coffee is on point.  They also do some workshops to talk about freshness and different types of coffees. But beside the coffee they are a cute little shop with giftables, clothing, bags, books, kids clothes and items, jewelry and much more.  Since I'm here so often it doesn't get boring...they are always changing the merchandise and updating products. They are part of the five stars app. Which helps you earn points to free and discounted products, special rewards and events.   Staff are pretty frendly as well.  Hope they keep it up!<//review>

<Text>I took my truck to the Lancaster Grand American Tire (GAT) to get new tires, shocks, and upper control arms put on.

The truck is a 1995 Dodge 2500 4x4.

The tires and shocks were provided by GAT, I brought the control arms because I could only find one company that makes them cnc bent to clear larger tires without rubbing. I put the lowers on myself.

The upper bolts were difficult to remove so I supplied new bolts and nuts in case the old ones had to be cut out. Ramsey, the service advisor, told me they had to remove the lowers to get to the uppers and would charge an extra hour of labor, I understood, that was fine.

After GAT had the truck a full week I was told it's done. When I arrived (Friday 3/16) the control arms were installed with the bend pushing out so that the tires rubbed even more than stock.  When they took off the lowers that I already did they didn't even put them back on the same way. I was asked to take the truck and bring it back next week to be fixed.

Unfortunately I was moving that next week and I did not get the impression they would be able to fix it in time so I took it upon myself to flip all four control arms that weekend. Which I did. Ramsey also told me they had quite a bit of trouble installing them, but I was able to do it with a pair of jack stands and a basic tool kit without trouble...

What I found was disappointing to say the least. The upper control arms had been considerably damaged by what I can only assume was an incompetent mechanic.  They had sustained numerous heavy blows from a pointed object leaving the surface heavily pocked. I don't see why this was necessary when a rubber mallet or dead blow hammer would have done the same job of maneuvering the control arm without damaging it. Each control arm also used to have a grease fitting at each end and three out of the four on the uppers were sheared off. I'm surprised that this was not mentioned to me upon delivery of the truck and even more surprised that they were not replaced with new fittings after being broken off. I also found that the nuts I supplied were not used. The drivers side at least had the old flanged nuts which is good, but the passenger side had a regular nut with no flange and no washer. So they seem to have lost enough nuts (at least 6) that they had to dig a couple out of a bucket somewhere, but to use a regular nut without a washer is unprofessional. I would have rather been told and charged the $5 for new nuts that were correct.

I have attached pictures of the control arms how they installed them, and the damage I found when I took them off to flip them over correctly.  The last picture on the tailgate shows them with new grease fittings that I had to go buy and install.

They did check the alignment for me after I fixed their botched job.  I asked them for a refund for a portion of the labor I paid for, since I didn't get what I paid for, but got nothing.</Text><Pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNhWWyBsgttlP7N7zoELixqgMYs8tK3vXaZ8RGa=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOg6KTdlES7BdxBoVdRPbG6hwDqL3hq3vYylopj=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMs24pJfxwWvRiJDBNB3cbD1rr7tf5p4tkPwwsV=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN331k9t6ce256WA09x_PnF5CDtawUysrnUHLwg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOuL1l8qaXCFaLEgvBUERYED420ISfPVRyoILZH=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO8f9jDPwaVBPdCn24RWH4usgFecvyxqhD9CKMh=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//Pics><response>None<//response><gmap_id>0x80c25ac10bc08f79:0x2da490231b302bdf</gmap_id></record>
